NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

A. WILLIAM NATHANIEL,

SIMULATION TECHNOLOGY SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED

Registered Office: No. 89, “T” Block, Anna Nagar, Chennai-600 040.
Notice pursuant to section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, is hereby given for general information, that the Members
of SIMULATION TECHNOLOGY SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED, at the Annual General Meeting of the Company held on
1st July 2015 at its Registered office of the Company, have passed the following special resolution to wind up the above
said Company by Members’ Voluntary Winding up.
Members’ Voluntary winding up of the Company:
“RESOLVED that having regard to the declaration made by the Board of Directors dated 10-6-2015 and delivered to
the Registrar under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956 (including any statutory modification, amendment or
supersession thereof) and applicable and notified provisions of the Companies Act, 2013 stating that the company will be
able to pay its debts in full within a reasonable period of time from the date of commencement of winding-up on the date
of declaration hereof, the Company having its Registered office at No.89, “T”-Block, Anna Nagar, Chennai-600 040, be
wound up voluntarily as Members’ Voluntary winding-up pursuant to Section 484(1)(b) and other relevant provisions if any
of the Companies Act, 1956 and any statutory modification thereof ”.
Chennai, 9th July 2015.

Simulation Technology Services Private Limited.
Dr. S. MOHAN,
Liquidator.
